The Load() function orchestrates the entire configuration loading chain by calling loadConfiguration(). loadConfiguration() performs the following steps in order: (1) loads conf/defaults.ini using gopkg.in/ini.v1 package, (2) applies command-line default properties via applyCommandLineDefaultProperties(), (3) loads custom config file via loadSpecifiedConfigFile(), (4) applies environment variable overrides via applyEnvVariableOverrides(), (5) applies command-line properties via applyCommandLineProperties(), and (6) evaluates config values containing environment variables via expandConfig(). I've completed a comprehensive analysis of Grafana's configuration loading system and created the answer file. Here's a summary of what I found:\n\n## Key Findings\n\n**Configuration Loading Architecture:**\n\nThe configuration system in Grafana uses an INI file parser (gopkg.in/ini.v1) with multiple levels of overrides. The main files are:\n\n1. **pkg/setting/setting.go** - Core configuration handling with:\n   - `Cfg` struct managing all configuration state\n   - `Load()` method orchestrating the configuration loading chain\n   - `loadConfiguration()` implementing the multi-step override process\n   - `applyEnvVariableOverrides()` for environment variable overrides (GF_SECTION_KEY format)\n   - `RedactedValue()` for masking sensitive configuration values\n\n2. **pkg/setting/provider.go** - Provider interface and OSSImpl implementation:\n   - `Provider` interface for configuration access\n   - `SettingsBag` and `VerboseSettingsBag` types for settings representation\n   - `Current()` method exposing settings with sensitivity masking\n\n3. **pkg/setting/expanders.go** - Configuration value expansion:\n   - `expandConfig()` for evaluating environment variables and file references\n   - Support for `${VAR_NAME}` and `$__file{path}` patterns\n\n4. **pkg/api/admin.go** - /api/admin/settings endpoint:\n   - `AdminGetSettings()` exposing configuration via HTTP API\n   - `getAuthorizedSettings()` filtering based on access control\n\n5. **conf/defaults.ini** - Default configuration values per section\n\n**Configuration Override Chain:**\n1.
